Hydrogen Bonding: The NH groups of the pyrrole rings can act as hydrogen bond donors, forming strong hydrogen bonds with the anion (especially if the anion is basic, such as chloride, acetate, or phosphate).\n\n2. Electrostatic Interactions: The negative charge of the anion is attracted to the partial positive charges on the hydrogen atoms of the pyrrole NH groups, as well as any other electron-deficient sites on the calixarene framework.\n\n3.
